              <h2 class="article-section-title">

                <h3 class="entry-title">

             <div class="wp-block-group__inner-container">
              <h4 class="has-white-color has-text-color" id="h-college-journalism-network">
               College Journalism Network
              </h4>
              <p class="has-white-color has-text-color amp-wp-0cf08eb" data-amp-original-style="font-size:14px">

              </p>

               </a>

              <h2 class="article-section-title">
               <span>
                <a href="https://calmatters.org/category/commentary/">
                 Commentary
                </a>
               </span>
              </h2>
              <article class="tag-capitol-park tag-catholic-church tag-commentary tag-father-junipero-serra tag-juan-de-onate tag-junipero-serra tag-junipero-serra-statue tag-reader-reactions category-commentary category-justice category-reader-reactions type-post post-has-image" data-post-id="169659">
               <div class="entry-wrapper">
                <h3 class="entry-title">
                 <a href="https://calmatters.org/commentary/reader-reactions/2021/03/public-statues-of-unprincipled-leaders-should-be-taken-down/" rel="bookmark">
                  Public statues of unprincipled leaders should be taken down
                 </a>
                </h3>
                <p>
                 Public statues and streets named for brutal and unprincipled leaders like Junípero Serra carry shame for all of us and should be removed.
                </p>
               </div>
               <!-- .entry-wrapper -->
              </article>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
